<script>
    function receive_event(event) {
        var data = event.data,
            origin = event.origin;
        if (data == 'Oauth') {
            ADRApplication.emit('modal/user/login/show');
        }
        else if(data=='OauthClose')
        {
            var resetLoginImage = new Image();
            resetLoginImage.src = globalData.user.userUrl;
            resetLoginImage.onload = function(){
                window.location.href = '/dang-ky-mo-the';
            }
            resetLoginImage.onerror = function(){
                window.location.href = '/dang-ky-mo-the';
            }
        }
        else if(data=='OauthHome'){
            bootbox.hideAll();            
        }
        else if(data=='vgc_reg_done')
        {
            if(dataLayer!==undefined){
                dataLayer.push({
                    event: "vgc_reg_done"
                });
            }
        }
        else if(data=='OauthConnect'){
            window.parent.location.href = 'https://authen.adayroi.com/VinCard/UserCardInfo?st=o';
        }
        else if(data=='OauthInfo'){
            window.parent.location.href = '/vingroupcard';
        }
        else if(data=='OauthRegister'){
            bootbox.hideAll();
            ADRApplication.emit('modal/iframe/create', {
                url: globalData.urls.register,
                className: 'modal-register'
            });
        }
    };

    $(document).ready(function(){
        if (window.addEventListener) {
            window.addEventListener("message", receive_event, false);
        }
        else {
            if (window.attachEvent) {
                window.attachEvent("onmessage", receive_event, false);
            }
        }
    });
</script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        (function(){
            var isUpdated = $.cookie('isUpdated');

            if(!isUpdated){
                var cityKey = globalData.user.cookieKeys.cityId,
                    districtKey = globalData.user.cookieKeys.districtId,
                    wardKey = globalData.user.cookieKeys.wardId,
                    displayTextKey = globalData.user.cookieKeys.displayText;

                var cookieSettings = globalData.user.cookieSettings;

                var cityVal = $.cookie(cityKey),
                    districtVal = $.cookie(districtKey),
                    wardVal = $.cookie(wardKey),
                    displayTextVal = $.cookie(displayTextKey);

                if(cityVal){
                    $.cookie(cityKey, cityVal, cookieSettings);
                }
                if(districtVal){
                    $.cookie(districtKey, districtVal, cookieSettings);
                }
                if(wardVal){
                    $.cookie(wardKey, wardVal, cookieSettings);
                }
                if(displayTextVal){
                    $.cookie(displayTextKey, displayTextVal, cookieSettings);
                }

                $.cookie('isUpdated', true, cookieSettings);
            }
        })();
    </script>
